Method: 提出LIFE四阶段框架：Lay（构建能力基础）、Integrate（通过协作集成智能体）、Find（通过归因发现故障）、Evolve（通过自主改进进化）。为每阶段提供系统化分类，形式化刻画相邻阶段的依赖关系，并识别跨阶段边界的开放问题。

Result: 给出了LIFE框架的系统化综述，定义了各阶段的分类体系，揭示了阶段间的因果约束链，并指出了现有工作在阶段边界处的不足，例如故障归因如何反馈到能力重建和协作重组尚未得到有效解决。

Conclusion: 呼吁构建闭环多智能体系统，实现持续诊断失败、重组结构和优化行为，将当前协调框架推向更自组织的集体智能形式，为未来研究提供系统参考和概念路线图。

Abstract: LLM-based autonomous agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in reasoning, planning, and tool use, yet remain limited when tasks require sustained coordination across roles, tools, and environments. Multi-agent systems address this through structured collaboration among specialized agents, but tighter coordination also amplifies a less explored risk: errors can propagate across agents and interaction rounds, producing failures that are difficult to diagnose and rarely translate into structural self-improvement. Existing surveys cover individual agent capabilities, multi-agent collaboration, or agent self-evolution separately, leaving the causal dependencies among them unexamined. This survey provides a unified review organized around four causally linked stages, which we term the LIFE progression: Lay the capability foundation, Integrate agents through collaboration, Find faults through attribution, and Evolve through autonomous self-improvement. For each stage, we provide systematic taxonomies and formally characterize the dependencies between adjacent stages, revealing how each stage both depends on and constrains the next. Beyond synthesizing existing work, we identify open challenges at stage boundaries and propose a cross-stage research agenda for closed-loop multi-agent systems capable of continuously diagnosing failures, reorganizing structures, and refining agent behaviors, extending current coordination frameworks toward more self-organizing forms of collective intelligence. By bridging these previously fragmented research threads, this survey aims to offer both a systematic reference and a conceptual roadmap toward autonomous, self-improving multi-agent intelligence.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识图谱规模庞大，在问答和可视化等任务中难以处理；需要一种能够根据用户查询模式生成个性化摘要的方法，以仅保留相关信息，降低存储需求和查询运行时开销。

Method: 基于coreset理论，根据用户查询工作负载定义三元组的敏感度分数（重要性度量），通过基于敏感度的重要性采样从原图中抽取相关子集，确保子集与完整数据集的特性近似误差有界。

Result: 在Freebase、WikiData、DBpedia上的实验表明，COREKG在查询回答准确率和结构覆盖率上均优于GLIMPSE、PPR、iSummary、PEGASUS和APEX²等现有方法，且仅使用原始图的一小部分数据。

Conclusion: 基于coreset理论的个性化知识图谱摘要方法能够有效为不同用户生成适应其查询行为的小规模摘要，在保持高准确率的同时大幅降低存储和计算开销。

Abstract: Knowledge Graphs (KGs) are extensively used across different domains and in several applications. Often, these KGs are very large in size. Such KGs become unwieldy for tasks such as question answering and visualization. Summarization of KGs offers a viable alternative in such cases. Furthermore, personalized KG summarization is crucial in the current data-driven world as it captures the specific requirements of users based on their query patterns. Since it only maintains relevant information, the personalized summaries of KG are small, resulting in significantly smaller storage requirements and query runtime. In this work, we adapt the coreset theory to create personalized KG summaries. For a given dataset and a user-specific query workload, we present an approach that samples a relevant subset of triples using sensitivity-based importance sampling. We ensure that the subset approximates the characteristics of the full dataset with bounded approximation error. We define sensitivity scores that measure the importance of a triple with respect to a user's query workload, which are then used by our coreset construction algorithm. We explicitly focus on personalized knowledge graph summarization by constructing summaries independently for each user based on their query behaviour.
  Our evaluation on Freebase, WikiData, and DBpedia shows that COREKG delivers higher query-answering accuracy and structural coverage than the state-of-the-art methods, such as GLIMPSE, PPR, iSummary, PEGASUS and APEX$^2$ while requiring only a tiny fraction of the original graph.

</details>


### [301] [KGPFN: Unlocking the Potential of Knowledge Graph Foundation Model via In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14907)
*Yisen Gao,Jiaxin Bai,Haoyu Huang,Zhongwei Xie,Yufei Li,Hong Ting Tsang,Sirui Han,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出KGPFN，一种基于Prior-data Fitted Network的知识图谱基础模型，通过结合关系级迁移学习和结构化的上下文学习（包括局部邻居和全局关系实例），在57个基准上实现了优于微调方法的零样本适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KG基础模型主要强调关系层面的普适性，而忽视了上下文学习（ICL）这一基础模型的重要支柱。知识图谱中的上下文是结构化和异质的，现有方法未能有效利用推理时的结构化上下文信息。

Method: 1) 通过关系图上的消息传递学习跨图关系不变性表示；2) 使用多层NBFNet编码查询实体局部邻域作为局部上下文；3) 检索查询关系的大量实例及其局部邻域，构建关系特定的全局上下文；4) 在Prior-data Fitted Network框架中结合特征级和样本级注意力进行聚合；5) 多图预训练学习何时实例化可复用模式或根据上下文覆盖它们。

Result: 在57个KG基准上，KGPFN仅通过上下文学习就能在未见过的图上实现强适应能力，持续优于经过微调的有竞争力的KG基础模型。

Conclusion: KGPFN成功统一了可迁移的关系规律性与推理时的结构化上下文学习，为KG基础模型提供了一种新的范式。

Abstract: Knowledge graph (KG) foundation models aim to generalize across graphs with unseen entities and relations by learning transferable relational structure. However, most existing methods primarily emphasize relation-level universality, while in-context learning, the other pillar of foundation models remains under-explored for KG reasoning. In KGs, context is inherently structured and heterogeneous: effective prediction requires conditioning on the local context around the query entities as well as the global context that summarizes how a relation behaves across many instances. We propose KGPFN, a KG foundation model using Prior-data Fitted Network that unifies transferable relational regularities with inference-time in-context learning from structured context. KGPFN first learns relation representations via message passing on relation graphs to capture cross-graph relational invariances. For query-specific reasoning, it encodes local neighborhoods using a multi-layer NBFNet as local context. To enable ICL at global scale, it constructs relation-specific global context by retrieving a large set of instances of the query relation together with their local neighborhoods, and aggregates them within a Prior-Data Fitted Network framework that combines feature-level and sample-level attention. Through multi-graph pretraining on diverse KGs, KGPFN learns when to instantiate reusable patterns and when to override them using contextual evidence. Experiments on 57 KG benchmarks demonstrate that KGPFN achieves strong adaptation to previously unseen graphs through in-context learning alone, consistently outperforming competitive fine-tuned KG foundation models. Our code is available at https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/KGPFN.

### [302] [From Sycophantic Consensus to Pluralistic Repair: Why AI Alignment Must Surface Disagreement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14912)
*Varad Vishwarupe,Nigel Shadbolt,Marina Jirotka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文批判了当前多元对齐研究中仅依赖偏好聚合（如覆盖、导向、分布）的做法，指出RLHF模型在对话中表现出“谄媚式共识”——倾向于赞同用户、平滑冲突。作者引入Grice会话准则中的三种对话机制（范围界定、信号标记、修复），并提出“多元修复评分”（PRS）以区分原则性修正与屈服性投降，实验表明前沿模型在争议性价值提示上存在低修复质量问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多元对齐研究多聚焦于偏好聚合（覆盖、导向、分布），但作者认为这种单一策略在面对真实价值多元主义时存在致命缺陷：RLHF训练出的模型倾向于对用户“谄媚式共识”，在健康、公民生活、劳动、治理等重大对话中介场景中，这种对分歧的抹杀具有分配性后果。因此需要从聚合转向会话机制层面的多元对齐。

Method: 基于Grice会话准则，提出三种对话机制：（1）范围界定（承认自身视角局限）；（2）信号标记（表面化价值冲突而非掩盖）；（3）修复（基于原则修正立场，而非迫于用户压力）。形式化定义“多元修复评分”（PRS），区分原则性修正与屈服性投降。在两个前沿RLHF模型（Claude Sonnet 4.5, N=198; GPT-4o, N=100）上进行小规模实证。

Result: 两个模型在争议性价值提示上均表现出“同意跟随”与“低修复质量”并存的现象。PRS揭示了模型在互动层面缺乏可见分歧与原则性修正的能力，表明现有对齐方法未能支撑会话层面的多元主义前提条件。

Conclusion: 多元主义最关键的成败发生在部署-治理层面（界面、偏好数据管道、审计基础设施），而非仅靠聚合方法。PRS测量的是多元主义的互动前提条件（可见分歧、原则性修正），而非完整的多元主义实现；作者也坦诚反思了“谁的原则算作原则”这一反身性问题。

Abstract: Pluralistic alignment is typically operationalised as preference aggregation: producing responses that span (Overton), steer toward (Steerable), or proportionally represent (Distributional) diverse human values. We argue that aggregation alone is an incomplete primitive for deployed pluralistic alignment. Under genuine value pluralism, the failure mode of contemporary RLHF-trained assistants is not insufficient coverage but sycophantic consensus: a learned tendency to agree with, validate, and minimise friction with the immediate interlocutor. Because deployed AI systems now mediate consequential deliberation across health, civic life, labour, and governance, the collapse of disagreement at the interaction layer is not a narrow technical concern but a structural failure with distributive consequences. We reframe pluralistic alignment around three conversational mechanisms drawn from Grice's maxims: scoping (acknowledging the limits of one's perspective), signalling (surfacing value-conflict rather than smoothing it over), and repair (revising one's position on principled grounds, not on user pressure). We formalise a metric, the Pluralistic Repair Score (PRS), distinguishing principled revision from capitulation, and present a small-scale empirical illustration on two frontier RLHF-trained models (Claude Sonnet 4.5, N=198; GPT-4o, N=100) showing that, for both, agreement-following coexists with low repair-quality on contested-value prompts. PRS measures an interactional precondition for pluralism (visible disagreement; principled revision) rather than pluralism in full; we discuss the difference, take seriously the reflexive question of whose "principled" counts, and argue that pluralism is most decisively made or unmade at the deployment-governance layer: interfaces, preference-data pipelines, and audit infrastructure.

</details>


### [303] [GraphFlow: An Architecture for Formally Verifiable Visual Workflows Enabling Reliable Agentic AI Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14968)
*Drewry H. Morris,Luis Valles,Reza Hosseini Ghomi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GraphFlow 是一个将工作流图作为可执行规范的可视化工作流系统，旨在提升多步骤、关键任务中 AI 自动化的可靠性。通过编译时形式化验证与运行时持久化执行引擎，在一年期临床试点中实现了 97.08% 的完成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多步骤工作流中，每步 90% 可靠性的十步流程仅有 35% 的成功率，小错误会迅速累积。现有工作流平台缺乏语义正确性保证，而智能体系统推理时规划易受提示变化影响且难以审计。GraphFlow 旨在弥补这一差距。

Method: 将工作流图视为可执行规范（单一工件定义数据范围、执行语义和监控）；编译时对受限类图进行规约，产生可复用自动化，其契约（前置条件、后置条件、组合义务）在入库前经证明检查；运行时持久化引擎将结果记录在仅追加事件日志中，可在系统边界执行契约，支持重放、重试和审计；泳道图明确信任边界，分离验证逻辑与外部系统、人工判断和 AI 决策。

Result: 在三个临床站点为期一年的试点中，早期原型（无验证核心子系统）执行了 8,728 次队列入组工作流，完成率达 97.08%；观察到的失败主要局限在外部集成。

Conclusion: GraphFlow 通过工作流图作为可执行规范结合形式化契约验证，能显著提升复杂代理工作流的可靠性。形式化语义和证明检查的准入模型已明确规范并在积极开发中，验证核心的评估留待未来工作。

Abstract: GraphFlow is a visual workflow system designed to improve the reliability of agentic AI automation in multi-step, mission-critical processes. In these workflows, small errors compound rapidly: under an idealized model of independent steps, a ten-step process with 90% per-step reliability completes successfully only 35% of the time. Existing workflow platforms provide durable execution and observability but offer few semantic correctness guarantees, while agentic systems plan at inference time, making behavior sensitive to prompt variation and difficult to audit.
  GraphFlow is designed to address this gap by treating workflow diagrams as the executable specification, a single artifact defining data scope, execution semantics, and monitoring. At compile time, a restricted class of diagrams is specified to produce reusable automations whose contracts (preconditions, postconditions, and composition obligations) are intended to be proof-checked before admission to a shared library. At runtime, a durable engine records outcomes in an append-only event log and can enforce contracts at system boundaries, supporting replay, retries, and audit. Swimlanes make trust boundaries explicit, separating verified logic from external systems, human judgment, and AI decisions.
  A year-long pilot across three clinical sites executed 8,728 cohort-enrolled workflow runs with a 97.08% completion rate under an early prototype without the verified-core subsystem; observed failures were localized primarily to external integrations. The formal semantics and proof-checked admission model described here are specified and under active development. Evaluation of the verified core is reserved for future work.

</details>


### [304] [Learning Developmental Scaffoldings to Guide Self-Organisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14998)
*Milton L. Montero,Elias Najarro,Jakob Schauser,Sebastian Risi*

TL;DR: 该研究通过神经细胞自动机（NCA）结合坐标基模式生成器（SIREN）联合学习自组织规则与初始预模式，发现将信息卸载到初始条件中可提升鲁棒性、编码容量和对称破缺能力，且有效预模式并非简单地近似目标，而是通过偏置发育动力学来促进收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界中许多系统通过自组织产生复杂结构，但大量信息实际上被卸载到初始条件中（如母体预模式）。作者希望理解这种信息卸载现象，并探究自组织规则与初始预模式之间的信息分布与协作机制。

Method: 提出一个联合学习框架：神经细胞自动机（NCA）学习自组织规则，SIREN网络作为坐标基模式生成器学习预模式，两者同时训练以生成目标图案。通过信息论分析测量信息在预模式与自组织过程之间的分布。

Result: 联合学习相比纯自组织方法在鲁棒性、编码容量和对称破缺方面均有提升。信息论分析表明有效预模式并非直接近似目标，而是通过偏置发育动力学促进收敛。

Abstract: From subcellular structures to entire organisms, many natural systems generate complex organisation through self-organisation: local interactions that collectively give rise to global structure without any blueprint of the outcome. Yet a significant portion of the information driving such processes is not produced by self-organisation itself, instead, it is often offloaded to initial conditions of the system. Biological development is a prime example, where maternal pre-patterns encode positional and symmetry-breaking information that scaffolds the self-organising process. From maternal morphogen gradients in early embryogenesis to tissue-level morphogenetic pre-patterns guiding organ formation, this transfer of information to initial conditions, analogous to a memory-compute trade-off in computational systems, is a fundamental part of developmental processes. In this work, we study this offloading phenomenon by introducing a model that jointly learns both the self-organisation rules and the pre-patterns, allowing their interplay to be varied and measured under controlled conditions: a Neural Cellular Automaton (NCA) paired with a learned coordinate-based pattern generator (SIREN), both trained simultaneously to generate a set of patterns. We provide information-theoretic analyses of how information is distributed between pre-patterns and the self-organising process, and show that jointly learning both components yields improvements in robustness, encoding capacity, and symmetry breaking over purely self-organising alternatives. Our analysis further suggests that effective pre-patterns do not simply approximate their targets; rather, they bias the developmental dynamics in ways that facilitate convergence, pointing to a non-trivial relationship between the structure of initial conditions and the dynamics of self-organisation.

*Rongman Xu,Yifei Li,Tianzhe Zhao,Yanrui Wu,Bo Li,Hang Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出双维度一致性（DDC）框架，通过置信度加权贝叶斯协议与趋势感知分层剪枝，在推理时实现采样广度与深度的统一优化，以10倍以上token消耗降低维持或提升LLM推理质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DDC框架，包含两个核心组件：1) 置信度加权贝叶斯协议（Confidence-Weighted Bayesian Protocol），用于评估推理路径质量；2) 趋势感知分层剪枝（Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning），实现自适应终止，将计算资源集中于高质量推理路径。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in reasoning. However, maximizing their potential through inference-time scaling faces challenges in trade-off between sampling budget and reasoning quality. Current strategies remain inefficient as they typically treat sampling width and depth as orthogonal objectives, where width consensus methods risk reinforcing hallucinations, while depth pruning mechanisms prematurely truncate complex yet valid reasoning chains. Therefore, we propose Dual-Dimensional Consistency (DDC), a unified framework that bridges path quality with adaptive termination. By coupling Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol with a Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning, our method ensures that computational resources are concentrated on high quality reasoning paths, filtering hallucinations while accelerating consensus. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过控制消融实验，对引用的和未引用的图谱实体进行隔离、移除和遮蔽操作，比较这些操作对答案变化和准确性的影响。

Result: 引用的证据通常是必要的，因为移除它会显著改变答案并降低准确性；但引用并不充分，因为准确答案也可能依赖于未引用的遍历上下文和周围图谱结构。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation can improve factuality by grounding answers in external evidence, but Agentic GraphRAG complicates what it means for citations to be faithful. In these systems, an agent explores a knowledge graph before producing an answer and a small set of citations. We frame citation faithfulness as a trajectory-level problem: final citations should not only support the answer, but also account for the graph traversal, structure, and visited-but-uncited entities that may influence it. Through controlled ablation experiments, we compare the effects of isolating, removing, and masking cited and uncited graph entities. Our results show that cited evidence is often necessary, as removing it substantially changes answers and reduces accuracy. However, citations are not sufficient, because accurate answers can also depend on uncited traversal context and surrounding graph structure. These findings suggest that citation evaluation in Agentic GraphRAG should move beyond source support toward provenance over the broader retrieval trajectory.

### [308] [OpenDeepThink: Parallel Reasoning via Bradley--Terry Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15177)
*Shang Zhou,Wenhao Chai,Kaiyuan Liu,Huanzhi Mao,Qiuyang Mang,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OpenDeepThink 提出了一种基于 Bradley-Terry 成对比较的群体测试时计算框架，通过多轮生成、成对评判和自然语言变异来提升 LLM 推理能力，将 Gemini 3.1 Pro 的 Codeforces Elo 提升了 405 分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时计算扩展方法主要通过延长单条推理链来扩展深度，而并行采样多个候选虽然简单，但缺乏无真实标签验证器时的最佳候选选择机制，因为点式 LLM 评判存在噪声和偏差。

Method: 采用群体进化算法：每一代中 LLM 对随机配对的候选进行成对比较，通过 Bradley-Terry 模型聚合投票得到全局排名；保留排名靠前的候选，对前四分之三的候选使用比较过程中生成的自然语言批评进行变异，丢弃后四分之一的候选。

Result: 在八轮 LLM 调用（约 27 分钟）内，将 Gemini 3.1 Pro 的有效 Codeforces Elo 提升了 405 分。该方法可跨不同强弱模型迁移，无需重新调参。在多领域 HLE 基准上，增益集中在客观可验证领域，在主观领域效果相反。

Conclusion: OpenDeepThink 通过成对比较的群体搜索有效解决了无真实标签时的候选选择瓶颈，提供了一种既扩展深度又扩展宽度的测试时计算扩展方案，且具备跨模型迁移能力。

Abstract: Test-time compute scaling is a primary axis for improving LLM reasoning. Existing methods primarily scale depth by extending a single reasoning trace. Scaling breadth by sampling multiple candidates in parallel is straightforward, but introduces a selection bottleneck: choosing the best candidate without a ground-truth verifier, since pointwise LLM judging is noisy and biased. To address this, we introduce OpenDeepThink, a population-based test-time compute framework that selects via pairwise Bradley-Terry comparison. Each generation, the LLM judges random pairs of candidates and aggregates votes via Bradley-Terry into a global ranking; top-ranked candidates are preserved and the top three quarters are mutated using the natural-language critiques produced during comparison; the bottom quarter is discarded. OpenDeepThink raises Gemini 3.1 Pro's effective Codeforces Elo by +405 points in eight sequential LLM-call rounds (~27 minutes wall-clock). The pipeline transfers across weaker and stronger models without retuning, and on the multi-domain HLE benchmark, gains appear concentrated in objectively verifiable domains and reverse in subjective ones. We release CF-73, a curated set of 73 expert-rated Codeforces problems with International Grandmaster annotation and 99% local-evaluation agreement against the official verdict.

</details>

### [309] [Realiz3D: 3D Generation Made Photorealistic via Domain-Aware Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13852)
*Ido Sobol,Kihyuk Sohn,Yoav Blum,Egor Zakharov,Max Bluvstein,Andrea Vedaldi,Or Litany*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: Realiz3D提出一种轻量级框架，通过在扩散模型中显式解耦视觉域（真实/合成）与控制信号，利用小残差适配器学习域协变量，从而在保持3D一致性的同时生成更逼真的图像，有效缓解了合成渲染带来的视觉域差距问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通过微调预训练图像生成器来学习几何、材质、视角等控制信号，但由于合成渲染与真实照片之间存在域差距，导致生成图像的真实感下降。作者认为根本原因在于模型将控制信号的存在与合成外观建立了非预期的关联。

Method: 提出Realiz3D框架，核心思想是引入一个协变量（co-variate）来显式分离视觉域（真实/合成）与其他控制信号的学习。该协变量通过小型残差适配器注入模型，专门负责域迁移。另外，还利用对扩散模型中不同层和去噪步骤角色的深入理解，设计了新的训练和推理策略以增强控制信号向真实域的可迁移性。

Result: 在文本到多视图生成以及基于3D输入的纹理生成任务上，Realiz3D能够生成同时具备3D一致性和高度真实感的图像，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 通过解耦控制信号与视觉域的学习，可以有效地在保持可控性的同时消除合成域带来的真实感损失，为3D一致图像生成提供了一种更实用的范式。

Abstract: We often aim to generate images that are both photorealistic and 3D-consistent, adhering to precise geometry, material, and viewpoint controls. Typically, this is achieved by fine-tuning an image generator, pre-trained on billions of real images, using renders of synthetic 3D assets, where annotations for control signals are available. While this approach can learn the desired controls, it often compromises the realism of the images due to domain gap between photographs and renders. We observe that this issue largely arises from the model learning an unintended association between the presence of control signals and the synthetic appearance of the images. To address this, we introduce Realiz3D, a lightweight framework for training diffusion models, that decouples controls and visual domain. The key idea is to explicitly learn visual domain, real or synthetic, separately from other control signals by introducing a co-variate that, fed into small residual adapters, shifts the domain. Then, the generator can be trained to gain controllability, without fitting to specific visual domain. In this way, the model can be guided to produce realistic images even when controls are applied. We enhance control transferability to the real domain by leveraging insights about roles of different layers and denoising steps in diffusion-based generators, informing new training and inference strategies that further mitigate the gap. We demonstrate the advantages of Realiz3D in tasks as text-to-multiview generation and texturing from 3D inputs, producing outputs that are 3D-consistent and photorealistic.

</details>


### [310] [FaceParts: Segmentation and Editing of Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13853)
*Tymoteusz Zapała,Julia Farganus,Dominik Galus,Mikołaj Czachorowski,Piotr Syga,Przemysław Spurek*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: FaceParts提出了一种无需监督即可对3D高斯泼溅虚拟化身进行面部部件分割和编辑的方法，支持跨化身部件交换，在NeRSemble数据集上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有面部编辑方法多基于2D图像生成模型或需人工编辑的3D网格辅助方法，缺乏直接对3D高斯泼溅化身进行无监督分割和编辑的方案。

Method: 提出FaceParts框架，直接在3D高斯域中操作，通过特征解缠、基于密度的聚类和FLAME锚定的部件迁移，实现无监督的面部语义部件分割与编辑。

Result: 在NeRSemble数据集11个主体上成功分离胡须、眉毛、眼睛和胡子等特征。部件迁移后身份一致性0.943，平均表情距离0.021，平均姿态距离0.004。

Conclusion: FaceParts实现了无需监督的3D高斯泼溅化身面部部件分割与编辑，且迁移部件能良好适应目标化身的姿态和表情，保持身份一致性。

Abstract: Facial editing is an important task with applications in entertainment, virtual reality, and digital avatars. Most existing approaches rely on generative models in the 2D image domain, while in 3D the task is typically performed through labor-intensive manual editing. We propose FaceParts, a framework for unsupervised segmentation and editing of Gaussian Splatting avatars. Unlike existing 2D or mesh-assisted methods, our approach operates directly in the Gaussian domain, decomposing avatars into semantically coherent facial parts without supervision. The method integrates feature disentanglement, density-based clustering, and FLAME-anchored part transfer, enabling precise editing and cross-avatar part swapping. Experiments on the NeRSemble dataset with 11 subjects demonstrate robust isolation of features such as beards, eyebrows, eyes and mustaches. Quantitative evaluation confirms that transferred segments adapt to pose and expression, while maintaining identity consistency (ID = 0.943), low Average Expression Distance (AED = 0.021) and low Average Pose Distance (APD = 0.004).

### [311] [SparseOIT: Improving Order-Independent Transparency 3DGS via Active Set Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13855)
*Wentao Yang,Fanzhen Kong,Zejian Kang,Xiangru Huang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出SparseOIT，一种基于顺序无关透明渲染的3D高斯泼溅重建算法，通过维护活跃高斯集合并利用稀疏性实现加速，在非朗伯/透明材质重建中优于现有OIT方法，性能媲美最先进的体渲染3DGS方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在非朗伯或透明材质对象上表现不佳，现有OIT方法虽尝试解决但潜力未被充分挖掘。

Method: SparseOIT通过维护一个活跃高斯集合，利用OIT渲染方程中变量依赖稀疏的特性，结合活跃集方法进行优化，并融入几何正则化。

Result: SparseOIT在OIT系列方法中大幅领先，且性能与基于体渲染的最先进3DGS重建方法相当。

Conclusion: SparseOIT有效利用了OIT渲染的稀疏性，在非朗伯/透明材质场景中实现了高效且高质量的重建。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has received tremendous popularity over the past few years due to its photorealistic visual appearance. However, 3DGS uses volumetric rendering that is not suitable for objects with non-lambertian or transparent materials. To remedy this issue, a family of Order-Independent Transparency (OIT) rendering methods propose to remove or modify the depth sorting step in the 3DGS rendering equation. However, the potential of OIT-based method is still underexplored. In this paper, we observe that the OIT modifications to the rendering equation significantly reduce the inter-independence among individual gaussian splats, resulting in very sparse variable dependencies that can be harnessed by specific optimization techniques such as active set method. To this end, we propose SparseOIT, an OIT-based 3DGS reconstruction algorithm that maintains an active set of gaussian splats and enjoys an acceleration ratio that is proportional to the potential sparsity. SparseOIT is designed by jointly considering the OIT rendering equation, the reconstruction algorithm and the geometric regularization. Through extensive experiments, we demonstrate that SparseOIT outperforms existing methods in the OIT-family by a large margin and also achieves comparable performance to the state-of-the-art 3DGS reconstruction methods based on volumetric rendering. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在海报设计中，布局至关重要，但专业设计师需为同一产品图像设计不同布局以满足不同用户需求，人工成本高。现有方法缺乏对用户自定义约束（如布局属性、部分布局）的灵活支持。

Method: 1）用不同均值的高斯噪声采样表示不同布局属性；2）提出属性一致性损失与属性解耦损失确保生成布局满足指定属性；3）设计局部约束损失以利用不完整的布局信息引导生成；4）引入随机掩码增强局部约束的多样性，促进模型学习更通用的潜在表示。

Conclusion: 该工作有效解决了海报布局生成中用户自定义约束的难题，通过属性解耦与局部约束机制实现了灵活可控的自动布局生成，具备实用价值。

Abstract: Graphic layout is essential in poster generation. Professionals often need to design different layouts for a product image, to ensure they meet specific user requirements. This paper focuses on utilizing a deep-learning model to automatically generate image-aware layouts with user-defined constraints, including layout attributes and partial layouts. Layout attribute constraints require generated layouts to include and exclude elements of specified classes, such as text, logos, underlays, and embellishments. Our model represents different attributes by sampling multidimensional Gaussian noise with different means, and we propose an attribute-consistent loss and an attribute-disentangled loss to ensure that the generated layout satisfies the specified attribute. Partial layout constraints provide our model with incomplete layout information to guide the generation of the remaining elements. We design a partial-constraint loss to incorporate the provided partial layout. Furthermore, we introduce a random mask to diversify the partial layout constraints, which can encourage the model to learn more general latent representations of the provided partial layouts. Both quantitative and qualitative evaluations demonstrate that our model can generate different image-aware layouts according to various user constraints while achieving state-of-the-art performance.

### [313] [MoZoo:Unleashing Video Diffusion power in animal fur and muscle simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13857)
*Dongxia Liu,Jie Ma,Xiaochen Yang,Jiancheng Zhang,Bin Xia,Zhehan Kan,Nisha Huang,Jun Liang,Wenming Yang,Jin Li*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: MoZoo 是一个生成式动力学求解器，能从粗糙网格生成高保真动物视频，包含 RAR-RoPE、非对称解耦注意力等创新模块，并构建了 MoZoo-Data 数据集和 MoZooBench 基准，在多种动物上实现了高质量的毛皮模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统影视级动物特效需要精确建模肌肉和毛发动态，既耗时又计算昂贵。虽然生成式扩散模型在艺术创作中表现出色，但其在高保真动物模拟方面的潜力尚未被开发。

Method: 提出 MoZoo 生成式动力学求解器：1) Role-Aware RoPE (RAR-RoPE) 通过基于角色的索引重映射同步运动对齐并解耦参考信息；2) 非对称解耦注意力机制分割潜在序列，强制单向信息流，防止特征干扰并提升计算效率；3) MoZoo-Data 合成到真实管线，利用渲染引擎和逆向映射构建大规模配对序列数据集。

Result: 实验表明 MoZoo 在多种动物骨架和布局上实现了高保真毛皮模拟，保持了优越的时间一致性和结构一致性，并在 MoZooBench 基准（120个网格-视频对）上验证了效果。

Conclusion: MoZoo 提供了从粗糙网格到高保真动物视频的端到端解决方案，绕过了传统精修流程，在动物特效生成领域展示了生成式模型的巨大潜力。

Abstract: The creation of cinematic-quality animal effects necessitates the precise modeling of muscle and fur dynamics, a process that remains both labor-intensive and computationally expensive within traditional production workflows. While generative diffusion models have shown promise in diverse artistic workflows, their capacity for high-fidelity animal simulation remains largely unexploited. We present MoZoo, a generative dynamics solver that bypasses conventional refinement to synthesize high-fidelity animal videos from coarse meshes under multimodal guidance. We propose Role-Aware RoPE (RAR-RoPE) which employs role-based index remapping to synchronize motion alignment while decoupling reference information via fixed temporal offsets. Complementing this, Asymmetric Decoupled Attention partitions the latent sequence to enforce a unidirectional information flow, effectively preventing feature interference and improving computational efficiency. To address the scarcity of high-quality training data, we introduce MoZoo-Data, a synthetic-to-real pipeline that leverages a rendering engine and an inverse mapping approach to construct a large-scale dataset of paired sequences. Furthermore, we establish MoZooBench, a comprehensive benchmark with 120 mesh-video pairs. Experimental results demonstrate that MoZoo achieves high-fidelity fur simulation across diverse animal skeletons and layouts, preserving superior temporal and structural consistency.

</details>


### [314] [Seed3D 2.0: Advancing High-Fidelity Simulation-Ready 3D Content Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13862)
*Diandian Gu,Jing Lin,Gaohong Liu,Jiahang Liu,Su Ma,Guang Shi,Jun Wang,Qinlong Wang,Qianyi Wu,Zhongcong Xu,Xuanyu Yi,Zihao Yu,Jianfeng Zhang,Zhuolin Zheng,Yifan Zhu,Rui Chen,Hengkai Guo,Xiaoyang Guo,Mingcong Han,Xu Han,Xiu Li,Yixun Liang,Weiqiang Lou,Junzhe Lu,Guan Luo,Minghan Qin,Shuguang Wang,Yuang Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 3D 生成系统在几何细节、材质真实感、以及面向物理仿真的场景级生成能力方面仍存在不足，Seed3D 2.0 旨在解决这些问题，提升生成保真度并扩展至可交互的场景构建。

Method: 1) 几何：粗到细两阶段流水线（全局结构学习 → 高频细节恢复）+ 局部感知 VAE（更高空间压缩与高效解码）；2) 纹理材质：统一 PBR 模型替代级联流水线，直接生成多视角反照率与金属-粗糙度图，引入 MoE 缩放和 VLM 语义条件；3) 仿真套件：场景布局规划、部件感知分解、无训练关节生成，支持物理引擎中的交互。

Result: 在带纹理 3D 资产生成任务中，与五个近期商业模型相比，Seed3D 2.0 的胜率为 69.0% 到 89.9%。

Conclusion: Seed3D 2.0 在生成质量、材质精度和仿真能力上全面优于 Seed3D 1.0 及当前主流商业模型，展现了从单物体生成到场景级物理交互的跨越式进步。

Abstract: We present Seed3D 2.0, an advanced 3D content generation system built on Seed3D 1.0, with substantial improvements across generation fidelity, simulation-ready capabilities, and application coverage. For geometry, a coarse-to-fine two-stage pipeline decouples global structure learning from high-frequency detail recovery, while a locality-aware VAE achieves higher spatial compression and more efficient decoding. For texture and material generation, we replace the cascaded pipeline of Seed3D 1.0 with a unified PBR model that directly generates multi-view albedo and metallic-roughness maps, enhanced by Mixture-of-Experts scaling and VLM-based semantic conditioning for improved material precision and visual fidelity. Beyond single-object generation, Seed3D 2.0 introduces a simulation-ready model suite comprising scene layout planning, part-aware decomposition, and training-free articulation generation, enabling coherent scene construction and part-level physical interaction across physics and graphics engines. A large-scale human preference study against five recent commercial models shows that Seed3D 2.0 achieves consistent win rates of 69.0% to 89.9% in textured 3D asset generation. ### [315] [Fast and Robust Mesh Simplification for Generated and Real-World 3D Assets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14029)
*Kunal Bhosikar,Preet Savalia,Lokender Tiwari,Brojeshwar Bhowmick*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出FA-QEM，一种面向现代3D资产的特征感知网格简化方法，通过多项二次误差度量联合优化几何偏差、边界曲率和法线一致性，在保持尖锐特征的同时实现高效简化，并在AI生成网格和真实数据集上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代3D重建和生成管线产生大量稠密、噪声且非流形的网格，这些网格对下游应用（仿真、AR/VR、科学计算）造成挑战，亟需一种快速、鲁棒且能保留精细几何结构与高质量外观的网格简化方法。

Method: 提出FA-QEM流水线，核心是新颖的多项二次误差度量，联合编码几何偏差、边界曲率和表面法线一致性，实现保留尖锐特征的最优顶点放置；简化后的几何作为前端，通过逐次映射技术提升纹理映射质量。

Result: 在AI生成网格、Thingi10K和真实世界纹理数据集上，FA-QEM在几何误差、视觉保真度和运行速度上均一致优于现有方法，对多样化输入具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: FA-QEM是一种实用且高效的组件，适用于可扩展的3D重建与生成管线，其几何简化能显著提升下游外观迁移效果。

Abstract: The rapid growth of 3D content from modern reconstruction and generative pipelines, such as neural rendering and large-scale 3D asset generation, has led to an abundance of dense, noisy, and often non-manifold meshes. While these representations achieve high visual fidelity, their complexity poses significant challenges for downstream applications in simulation, AR/VR, and scientific computing, where efficient and reliable geometry is essential. This necessitates mesh simplification methods that are not only fast and robust to "in-the-wild" inputs, but also capable of preserving fine geometric structures and high-quality appearance. In this paper, we propose Feature-Aware Quadric Error Metric (FA-QEM), a comprehensive mesh simplification pipeline designed for modern 3D assets. Our approach introduces a novel multi-term quadric error formulation that jointly encodes geometric deviation, boundary curvature, and surface normal consistency, enabling optimal vertex placement that preserves sharp features even under aggressive simplification. Furthermore, we show that high-fidelity geometric simplification significantly improves downstream appearance transfer, serving as a superior front-end for texture mapping via successive mapping techniques. We conduct extensive evaluations on both AI-generated meshes and large-scale real-world datasets, including Thingi10K and the Real-World Textured Things dataset. Our results demonstrate that FA-QEM achieves consistently lower geometric error, better visual fidelity, and substantially faster runtimes compared to existing methods, while maintaining robustness across diverse and challenging inputs. These properties make FA-QEM a practical and effective component for scalable 3D reconstruction and generation pipelines.

### [316] [DiffPhD: A Unified Differentiable Solver for Projective Heterogeneous Materials in Elastodynamics with Contact-Rich GPU-Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14526)
*Shih-Yu Lai,Sung-Han Tien,Jui-I Huang,Yen-Chen Tseng,Yi-Ting Chiu,Siyuan Luo,Ziqiu Zeng,Fan Shi,Peter Yichen Chen,Tiantian Liu,Yu-Lun Liu,Bing-Yu Chen*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: DiffPhD是一个统一的GPU加速可微投影动力学框架，通过刚度感知权重、信赖域特征值过滤、Anderson加速和统一GPU管线，能稳定高效处理异质材料、超弹性大变形和接触丰富的场景，在刚度对比度高达100倍的情况下仍保持收敛，速度提升一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可微仿真方法（如DiffPD）在处理真实世界中常见的异质材料刚度极端差异、超弹性大变形和丰富接触场景时面临困难，需要一种能同时解决这些相互交织挑战的统一框架。

Method: (i) 刚度感知投影权重将异质性嵌入全局系统；(ii) 信赖域特征值过滤用于反向传播稳定超弹性梯度，以及双门控收敛的II型Anderson加速稳定前向迭代；(iii) 统一GPU管线在正向、反向和接触计算中复用单个稀疏因子，将刚度放大的瑞利阻尼折叠进同一因子实现零额外成本的异质性感知耗散。

Result: 在异质、超弹性、接触丰富的基准测试上，DiffPhD实现了严格的梯度准确性，速度比之前的可微求解器提升一个数量级，且在刚度对比度高达100倍时仍保持收敛（而之前的方法会退化）。

Conclusion: DiffPhD解锁了端到端基于梯度的优化在之前因求解器脆弱性或每次迭代成本过高而受限的场景（如壳-关节复合生物、软体角色挥舞硬武器、软体夹爪机器人操作），所有场景均可在单个正向-反向传播中完成。

Abstract: Differentiable simulation of soft bodies is a foundation for system identification, trajectory optimization, and Real2Sim transfer. Yet, existing methods such as the differentiable Projective Dynamics (DiffPD) struggle when faced with heterogeneous materials with extreme stiffness contrasts, hyperelasticity under large deformations, and contact-rich interactions, which are common scenarios in the real world. We present DiffPhD, a unified GPU-accelerated differentiable Projective Dynamics framework for heterogeneous materials that tackles these intertwined challenges simultaneously. Our key insight is a careful integration of: (i) stiffness-aware projective weights to embed heterogeneity into the global system; (ii) trust-region eigenvalue filtering lifted to the backward pass for stable hyperelastic gradients and a type-II Anderson Acceleration scheme with dual-gate convergence to stabilize forward iteration under large stiffness contrasts; and (iii) a unified GPU pipeline that reuses a single sparse factor across forward, backward, and contact computations, with stiffness-amplified Rayleigh damping folded into the same factor for heterogeneity-aware dissipation at zero recurring cost. DiffPhD achieves strict gradient accuracy while delivering up to an order-of-magnitude speedup over prior differentiable solvers on heterogeneous, hyperelastic, contact-rich benchmarks. Crucially, this speedup does not come at the cost of stability: DiffPhD remains convergent on stiffness contrasts up to 100x where prior PD solvers degrade. This unlocks end-to-end gradient-based optimization on regimes previously bottlenecked by either solver fragility or per-iteration cost -- shell--joint composite creatures, soft characters wielding stiff weapons, and soft-gripper robotic manipulation -- all handled within a single forward--backward pass.

</details>


### [317] [AnchorRoute: Human Motion Synthesis with Interval-Routed Sparse Contro](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14716)
*Pengcheng Fang,Tengjiao Sun,Dongjie Fu,Xiaoyu Zhan,Yanwen Guo,Hansung Kim,Xiaohao Cai*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: AnchorRoute是一个基于稀疏锚点的运动合成框架，通过AnchorKV和双重上下文条件将稀疏锚点注入冻结的文本-运动扩散先验模型，生成完整人体运动；随后利用RouteSolver在锚点定义的区间基上进行残差细化，支持根轨迹、平面轨迹和身体关节点三种控制方式，在稀疏关键点协议下优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏锚点提供了一种紧凑的人体运动创作接口，但现有方法在生成质量与锚点约束遵从性之间难以兼顾。本文旨在构建一个统一的框架，使生成器保持预训练文本-运动先验的高质量，同时通过同一锚点结构实现高效的残差细化。

Method: 1) 生成阶段：将稀疏锚点转换为锚点条件特征，通过AnchorKV和双重上下文条件注入冻结的Transition Masked Diffusion先验；2) 细化阶段：RouteSolver利用锚点定义细化区间，将软标记更新投影到锚点定义的分段仿射区间基上，实现残差路由细化。

Result: 在稀疏关键点协议下，AnchorRoute优于先前的稀疏控制方法，并在根3D、平面根和身体关节点三种控制族中一致提升了锚点遵从性。

Conclusion: 所提的锚点条件生成器与RouteSolver细化是互补的：生成器保持文本-运动质量，RouteSolver提供了可控的路径以实现更强的锚点遵从性。

Abstract: Sparse anchors provide a compact interface for human motion authoring: users specify a few root positions, planar trajectory samples, or body-point targets, while the system synthesizes the full-body motion that completes the under-specified intent. We present AnchorRoute, a sparse-anchor motion synthesis framework that uses anchors as a shared scaffold for both generation and refinement. Before generation, AnchorRoute converts sparse anchors into anchor-condition features and injects the resulting condition memory into a frozen Transition Masked Diffusion prior through AnchorKV and dual-context conditioning. This preserves the generation quality of the pretrained text-to-motion prior while learning sparse spatial control. After generation, the same anchors are evaluated as residuals: their timestamps define refinement intervals, and their residuals determine where correction should be concentrated. RouteSolver then refines the motion by projecting soft-token updates onto anchor-defined piecewise-affine interval bases. This couples generation-time anchor conditioning with residual-routed refinement under one anchor scaffold. AnchorRoute supports root-3D, planar-root, and body-point control within the same formulation. In benchmark evaluations, AnchorRoute outperforms prior sparse-control methods under the sparse keyjoint protocol and consistently improves anchor adherence across control families. The results show that the learned anchor-conditioned generator and RouteSolver refinement are complementary: the generator preserves text-motion quality, while RouteSolver provides a controllable path toward stronger anchor adherence.

### [318] [UMo: Unified Sparse Motion Modeling for Real-Time Co-Speech Avatars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14731)
*Xiaoyu Zhan,Xinyu Fu,Chenghao Yang,Xiaohong Zhang,Dongjie Fu,Pengcheng Fang,Tengjiao Sun,Xiaohao Cai,Hansung Kim,Yuanqi Li,Jie Guo,Yanwen Guo*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: UMo 提出了一种统一稀疏运动建模架构，通过文本、音频和运动令牌的统一处理，结合空间稀疏 MoE 和时序稀疏关键帧设计，实现了实时、高保真的共语手势和面部动画生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么局限于单模态（仅音频）进行语音-动作对齐，未能充分利用大规模人体运动数据；要么受限于多模态模型的表征能力和吞吐量，难以同时实现高质量运动生成和实时性能。

Method: 提出 UMo 统一架构：1）将文本、音频、运动令牌统一为同一种公式化表示；2）空间稀疏 MoE（Mixture-of-Experts）框架；3）时序稀疏关键帧设计实现实时稠密重建；4）多阶段训练策略配合音频数据增强，提升声学多样性和语义一致性。

Result: 在低延迟和实时性能约束下，UMo 在定量和定性评估中均取得了优于现有方法的输出质量，实现了高保真的共语动画生成。

Conclusion: UMo 为实时高保真共语虚拟形象提供了一种实用解决方案，在严格延迟约束下仍能保持精细的语音-动作对齐。

Abstract: Speech-driven gestures and facial animations are fundamental to expressive digital avatars in games, virtual production, and interactive media. However, existing methods are either limited to a single modality for audio motion alignment, failing to fully utilize the potential of massive human motion data, or are constrained by the representation ability and throughput of multimodal models, which makes it difficult to achieve high-quality motion generation or real-time performance. We present UMo, a unified sparse motion modeling architecture for real-time co-speech avatars, which processes text, audio, and motion tokens within a unified formulation. Leveraging a spatially sparse Mixture-of-Experts framework and a temporally sparse, keyframe-centric design, UMo efficiently performs real-time dense reconstruction, enabling temporally coherent and high-fidelity animation generation for both facial expressions and gestures. Furthermore, we implement a multi-stage training strategy with targeted audio augmentation to enhance acoustic diversity and semantic consistency. Consequently, UMo preserves fine-grained speech-motion alignment even under strict latency constraints. Extensive quantitative and qualitative evaluations show that UMo achieves better output quality under low latency and real-time performance constraints, offering a practical solution for high-fidelity real-time co-speech avatars.

### [319] [Meschers: Geometry Processing of Impossible Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14960)
*Ana Dodik,Isabella Yu,Kartik Chandra,Jonathan Ragan-Kelley,Joshua Tenenbaum,Vincent Sitzmann,Justin Solomon*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出Meschers，一种基于离散外微积分理论的网格表示方法，能够无需切割或弯曲即可有效表示不可能物体（如埃舍尔作品中的几何构造），并支持几何处理、重光照、距离计算等下游图形应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不可能物体表示方法（切割或弯曲）会破坏局部几何或影响重光照与距离计算，缺乏一种既能忠实表示不可能物体又支持标准几何操作的计算机表示方法。

Method: 提出Meschers表示法，基于离散外微积分（discrete exterior calculus）理论构建网格结构，使不可能物体的几何可以在不改变局部几何或不弯曲深度轴的情况下进行表示和处理。

Result: 在多个示例应用中展示了Meschers支持平滑、重光照、距离计算等下游操作，并能实现不可能物体的逆向渲染。与切割和弯曲表示法进行了对比。

Conclusion: Meschers为不可能物体提供了一种理论上完备、实用上可行的表示方法，填补了计算机图形学在该领域的空白。

Abstract: Impossible objects, geometric constructions that humans can perceive but that cannot exist in real life, have been a topic of intrigue in visual arts, perception, and graphics, yet no satisfying computer representation of such objects exists. Previous work embeds impossible objects in 3D, cutting them or twisting/bending them in the depth axis. Cutting an impossible object changes its local geometry at the cut, which can hamper downstream graphics applications, such as smoothing, while bending makes it difficult to relight the object. Both of these can invalidate geometry operations, such as distance computation. As an alternative, we introduce Meschers, meshes capable of representing impossible constructions akin to those found in M.C. Escher's woodcuts. Our representation has a theoretical foundation in discrete exterior calculus and supports the use-cases above, as we demonstrate in a number of example applications. Moreover, because we can do discrete geometry processing on our representation, we can inverse-render impossible objects. We also compare our representation to cut and bend representations of impossible objects.

</details>
